Despite Crust being extremely busy on a Wednesday evening our server and other waitstaff were extremely friendly and helpful.  The Caprese salad was refreshing with the dressed arugula on the top in addition to the usual fresh mozzarella,  tomato slices and balsamic reduction. The pizza crust was crisp on the bottom with great texture and taste. First visit with the girlfriend. She had the cheese lasagna and I had the penne pasta. Food was very good, however it is not the quality or quantity e,elected for what they charge.  The service was horrible. We were seated within a few minutes of walking in, but it took 10 minutes just to get a drink order and the server was absent a large amount of the time. We had to wait long lengths of time for literally everything including drink refills, our food in general and even the check. We requested a takeout box and were brought it 15 minutes later and then had to wait another 15 minutes for the check.  Thus was during a slow time and not peak hours, so I see no excuse for the lack of service. I give this place food 3 1/2 stars out of 5, but the service is maybe 2 if I'm being generous.<//text>

< Text>
It just gets better & better. I started eating here shortly after it's opening about a year ago and was wowed by it's amazing pizza, the best I've had anywhere.  Well, that continues to be true and it doesn't stop there.  I fell in love with the spicy meatballs, the roasted artichoke appetizer, the spaghetti & meatballs and their host of lunch & dinner salads, all available with steak, chicken or my favorite, the new spicy blackened chicken.

Once again they've stepped up their game, adding amazing daily homemade soups and my absolute favorite ever salad, their "wedge".  It's a classic, with iceberg lettuce wedges (yes, plural...read HUGE), bacon, cherry tomatoes and a heavenly blue cheese dressing oozing around like white liquid gold. I top it with the blackened chicken and love it!  It's way too big but it doesn't stop me from eating the WHOLE thing, good thing I usually have a pal along to roll me out!

They also have a nice selection of craft beers and great wine at reasonable prices, all served by a young, cheerful & attractive staff.  So I only have two questions:

1. Can it get any better?
2. Why are you reading this when you could be there eating?

Now I've done it....I'm gettin' in my car and heading there NOW.<//Text>

<Name>David Guettler< /Name>< Text>
My time spent inside "Crust" was less than 5 minutes. I simply picked up a pizza to go.  I inhaled the environment of "Crust" in those few minutes.

The 5 stars I gave was 95 percent for the pizza and 5 percent for my short experience inside and over the phone ordering.

If your a serious pizza lover that appreciates quality and taste, this place is top tier for you.  Traveling often for business I get around the US and can tell you "Crust" is in the top 10 percent. (Been to NY and Chicago, interesting enough, and never had time to get pizza)

I created my own pizza.
I had a 10" pizza with Artisan crust (regular), Wisconsin mozzarella cheese, Portobello mushrooms, black olives and onions. My total was 14.85 and that was for two people. No complaints, your getting quality.  First and final opinion is this place has great pizza.  The only local pizza equal is "Marco's" in Vista, CA.

I will come here again, and I live in San Marcos 6 miles away.

The environment inside made me think i was inside"Chipotle" with servers and a bar added. That is not saying a bad thing. I am just  describing the inside as best I can. Wide beer and wine selection.  I interacted with three employees and they were all friendly. Others will probably disagree, but I PERSONALLY would not go there with a group bigger than 6. Customer service over the phone for the order was great. Plenty of parking.

Pizzaholic tourists getting the "shakes" should definitely go here if in Carlsbad, CA.</Text>

<text>What an experience!! The guys at go jump are super professional but fun and light hearted at the same time. At no point was I concerned about my safety or well being. We went as a group of 5, we pre booked online and once we got there it was a smooth check in process. We booked our jump for 2pm and were harnessed and ready to jump within half hour of our jump time. You have the option of paying extra for hand cam footage OR having an extra diver jump with you filming the entire jump for you. ($98 for hand cam & $128 for the extra diver). The jump itself was phenomenal. Seeing the ocean and skyline was absolutely breathtaking!! It was about 5ish mins in total. Be prepared to have a bit of ear pain on the decent, but once your ears pop your good to go!

I would definitely recommend this place to anyone interested in going skydiving. You're in good hands at go jump!</text>< Pics>

We had such a great time skydiving with GoJump Oceanside!! I went with my mom, brother, and friend who was the only person in our group who had completed a jump before. Our original booking was for a Sunday, however we weren‚Äôt able to jump because of the marine layer, which was still thick at 3pm. We rescheduled for 2 days later at 1pm. We arrived at 12:45pm and ended up jumping at 6:00pm. This was because of the same marine layer issue and it being a semi cloudy day. The staff were very friendly and great with keeping us informed and honest with their predictions on if there were going to be jumps that day. <text>For anyone wanting to go skydiving, this is it!  My pilot, Felix, was awesome, took great photos, and was always smiling.

This is toward the end of a long day.  I could easily see the whole crew was tired, but they kept the energy up as much as could be expected.  I give them a thumbs up!

Skydiving is an incredible sport and our goal is to share that with as many people as possible with a safe and incredible experience! Unfortunately, there are a few things that effect the safety of our favorite outdoor sport that are beyond our control- weather is one of them. Transition seasons (spring and fall) can sometimes bring a marine layer that will sit over the water and can move in and sit on top of our airspace making it unsafe to jump. Sometimes it clears up within minutes, sometimes it comes in and out, sometimes it sits there all day. Because the marine layer depends on outside versus water temperatures, they aren't on weather radars as clouds and can be very hard to predict or track. We do our absolute best to keep each of our customers informed as soon as we make decisions based on weather. Sometimes we nail it but other times the weather does something we didn't predict. Unfortunately those days you picked to jump, the weather wasn't operational. <Rate>2<//Rate>< Text>
All safety measures and precautions are taken, so there is no complaint about that from me. I appreciate that they don't take risks with safety. However, as many of the other reviews have mentioned, GoJump does not value the customer's time. They canceled our first appointment without notifying us, and we only found out after making the long drive down to the area. We rescheduled twice after that, and they were extremely inflexible about times. We had booked our first reservation about a month in advance, so they should have been more accommodating with their times.

The third reservation we booked was at 5 pm.  Remember, the time is booked with the assumption that you're actually going to be getting on the plane pretty soon after that time. We called at 3 to confirm that they were still on, and all seemed well. We arrived at 4:45 pm to be told that there was a 2 hour delay. We waited for an hour and 20 minutes, and then they canceled the rest of the jumps due to weather. There was no compensation for our wait, drive, or the inconvenience of constantly rescheduling.

Again, I'm glad that they don't try to force jumps in bad weather conditions, but this inefficient scheduling is ridiculous. I can't imagine trying to do this on a vacation with limited time. If you're really set on using this company, I'd suggest to book your reservation in the middle of the day and then plan to make it a full-day commitment.

When we finally did get to jump, it was truly an amazing experience. The tandem pilots are great and seem really focused on making sure you're comfortable.

In all, I think the office should be more organized and helpful. I think the best way to ensure your jump the first time is to schedule it for late morning or early afternoon. Thank you.<//Text>

<Rating>5<//Rating>< Text>
If it is your first time going skydiving and you would like to tandem skydive, I would recommend buying your ticket on Groupon. It is much cheaper. They are very nice people. It is usually somewhat crowded but the wait to go up is 30 minutes or less. The planes are always taking off to drop a new load of sky divers. They fully answer any questions you have and have great package deals for those who love skydiving. The area is calm. However, parking isn't that great. They also sell food outside while you wait. If you just want to watch, they have an area outside to watch.
Now when you go on the plane, they take you over the ocean. The instructors have GoPros to record every moment.
Appointments are required to secure your spot. They will cancel and reschedule due to weather. Make sure you check the weather if you don't wish to get an email or a call about them having to reschedule due to the weather.<//Text>

<text>Some friends and I made a reservation for a sunset jump (4pm), and drove out from las vegas to do it.  We left Vegas at 7 am, ready to go and with plenty of time to arrive, book our hotel, and head to skydive.  We got a text at 1 pm that day saying that our dive was canceled due to unforeseen circumstances.  We called, and were told that weather had pushed the timetable back, and if we wanted to come down they would try to fit us in, but no guarantees.

We decided to try our luck, and drove down...

We arrived at the office, and asked to speak to someone about whether we would be able to fly or not, they directed us to the manager who told us that at 8 am it had gotten very cloudy, and no one was able to jump for 3 hours.  As such the timetable had been pushed back, and sadly there was no time for us to jump today.  I explained we had driven all the way out from Las Vegas to jump with them, and he told us he understood that but there was nothing he could do, he offered to reschedule us for another day, but as they were full both Saturday and Sunday he was unwilling to schedule us for then.

The reasons for the low review score are these.

1.  The company did not call/text us when inclement weather occured to let us know we might be delayed.  Nor did they let us know after it was clear we WOULD be canceled (at 11 am)  They waited until 1pm to let us know.  I completely understand if things get canceled because of weather and am in no way holding them responsible for the weather.

2.  The company was unwilling to work with us in any way shape or form after bumping us from our times.  A reservation is a reservation, if someone has one for a specific time it holds no less value than someone from an earlier time.  If they are going to bump people who are later in favor of those who are earlier then it makes no sense whatsoever to EVER book later with these people.

3.  The company was perfectly willing to cancel later reservations, yet was unwilling to push anyone from other days in order to make things right with those who were canceled in prior days.

4.  While the manager displayed a calm demeanor, the receptionists don't.  They are rude, and unpleasant.

5.  If you say "I would like to make this right for you"  then do nothing whatsoever to "make this right for you"  then it is a lie.  Don't lie to potential customers.

We booked with Lake Elsinore skydiving the next day and had an awesome time.  its a little bit more spendy, but the customer service was good, and it actually felt like they cared.<//text>< pics>
